<div class="bsky-content" markdown="1">

my proposal for resolving the carousel situation if you have a github account, please give it a 👍 if you agree github.com/bluesky-social/social-app/issues/10339issuecomment-4304918324



<div class="bsky-image-grid bsky-grid-1" markdown="1">



![screenshot of GitHub comment by @surfdude29 in issue &#34;image carousel creates unnecessary friction for the user&#34; #10339  I&#39;m probably going to be a lone voice in this thread because I actually do rather like the carousel image viewer for some image sets. However, for other image sets I agree that the grid format works better.  The good news is that I think there&#39;s a way to keep most people happy on this issue by giving users a choice.  Here&#39;s what I propose:  - **All image sets posted before the latest update was released would continue to be displayed in grid format, because this was the only image display format available at the time and posts were made with this in mind.** This would only need a fairly simple code change.  - The current `images` embed format is planned to be replaced with a [new `gallery` embed format](https://github.com/bluesky-social/atproto/pull/4827), which will allow more than 4 images to be posted, and will also eventually allow mixing images and videos. - **In this new embed format, there is a great opportunity to add a `display` option that allows the post author to pick either `grid` or `carousel` display for the images in the post.** (This would only be relevant for posts that have 2, 3 or 4 images.)  Taken together, these two proposals would ensure that images posted before the carousel introduction are always viewed in grid format, and going forward the author of a post would be able to choose whether they want the 2, 3 or 4 images in their post to be displayed in either `grid` or `carousel` format. ](https://cdn.bsky.app/img/feed_fullsize/plain/did:plc:sflxm2fxohaqpfgahgdlm7rl/bafkreicnyvyvan7hgm7ccdfjw5hbwobxasmrfhrn3fuauoxdfbwzyauztq){ .bsky-img }
